msg:A hotel with excellent value for money - superb location, spacious, comfortable and clean rooms, great service
We (a couple from Germany and Hong Kong) visit Chengdu frequently for business & leisure as it is one of our favourite cities in China. We have always stayed at Rhombus - our favourite hotel in Chengdu!

Its location is superb - right opposite to the bustling Taikoo Li (directly connected to a metro station). The hotel offers a perfect blend of comfort and style, with spacious, comfortable and clean rooms equipped with modern amenities, fast wi-fi and thoughtful touches. The staff, under the leadership! of the manager, Mia, are warm and attentive, always ready to make us feel welcome. The breakfast buffet is delicious and varied, with fresh and local ingredients.

Overall, Rhombus in Chengdu offers great value for money & exceeds our expectations. We highly recommend it and we will definitely come back again & again!
